<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verrekken.html>verrekken</a> (17274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rekken.html>rekken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verrekken.html>verrekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overstretch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a muscle</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to refuse to do
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>Ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probeerde.html>probeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> hard <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verrekte.html>verrekte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>No matter how hard the farmer tried to get him to work, the donkey <b>refused</b> to.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***verrijken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verrijken.html>verrijken</a> (24002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijk.html>rijk</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verrijken.html>verrijken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to enrich
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Engelse <a href = vnd.unilang:scheikundige.html>scheikundige</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Joseph_Priestley" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Joseph Priestley">Joseph Priestley</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontdekte.html>ontdekte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rond.html>rond</a> 1770 <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:methode.html>methode</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> water <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koolzuur.html>koolzuur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verrijken.html>verrijken</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>The English chemist <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Joseph_Priestley" class="extiw" title="w:en:Joseph Priestley">Joseph Priestlely</a> discovered around 1770 a method to <b>enrich</b> water with carbonic acid.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verrijken.html>verrijken</a></b>
</p>

***vers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a> (3051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">versch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fersk</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*frisk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*friskaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*preysk-</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fris.html>fris</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frisch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">farsk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fresh</i>, Danish and Norwegian <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">fersk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verser.html>verser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verst.html>verst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fresh</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">versus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vers.html>vers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verzen.html>verzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:versje.html>versje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A verse, a stanza.</li>
<li>A short poem.</li>
<li>Verse <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">poetic form with fixed rhyme and <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A verse; a line, sentence or similarly short passage of a text, usually in prose.</li></ol>

***verschalken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschalken.html>verschalken</a> (52863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschalken.html>verschalken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to subjugate, to mislead, to outwit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schalk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scoundrel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschalken.html>verschalken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to eat up, to catch and eat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiteindelijk.html>Uiteindelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijgerin.html>tijgerin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> lichtovetige <a href = vnd.unilang:prooi.html>prooi</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verschalken.html>verschalken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">In the end the tigress managed to <b>capture and devour</b> her light-footed prey.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mislead, to fool</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch by means of cunning, to <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a>, to capture, to ensnare</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ambush</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***verschansen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschansen.html>verschansen</a> (58731)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schans.html>schans</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschansen.html>verschansen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fortify; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to surround with a defensive wall, to protect with a bastion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dig oneself in, to seek cover, to fortify one's position, to take a fortified position</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schans.html>schans</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verschansen.html>verschansen</a></b>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschijnen.html>verschijnen</a> (4243)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verschinen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schijnen.html>schijnen</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschijnen.html>verschijnen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to appear, show up
<dl><dd><i>Hope <a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>Diamant</a>: 45,52 <a href = vnd.unilang:karaat.html>karaat</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verscheen.html>verscheen</a></b> in 1830 in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:handel.html>handel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekocht.html>gekocht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bankier.html>bankier</a> H.Ph. Hope.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/DiamantBeroemde_diamanten">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Hope Diamond: 45.52 carat; appeared in business in 1830 and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> purchased by banker <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Phillip Hope.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be published
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verscheen.html>verscheen</a></b> in 1903, <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschouwd.html>beschouwd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:populaire.html>populaire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:inheemse.html>inheemse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschenen.html>verschenen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>This book, the first edition of which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> published in 1903, can be considered as the first popular book about native <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> to appear in the Dutch language.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***verschonen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschonen.html>verschonen</a> (12422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verschônen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, pure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verschonen.html>verschonen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to change, to replace with a clean piece of the same thing
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verschoon.html>verschoon</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lakens.html>lakens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regelmatig.html>regelmatig</a>.</i>  |  I <b>change</b> my bedsheets regularly.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to excuse, <a href = vnd.unilang:pardon.html>pardon</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to withhold, to fail to use or employ
